Huzhou 83

Misunderstanding Between Water Police and Home Guards: The Degu wheel of the Hushiban of the Changhang Bureau of this city was sailing from Sian back to this city on the 3rd of this month. It happened that Shen Arong, an investigator of the Bannan Home Guard, was also on the wheel back to the team. He glanced at the wheel and saw two bandits, each with a wooden shell gun. Shen Arong secretly instructed the helmsman to blow the whistle as a signal and stop the wheel. When passing near Tangkou, Shen Arong went ashore and ran to the team headquarters to report. The team chief, Liu Jingsheng, immediately led many armed team members to Tangkou after hearing the report. The sky was dark, Shen Arong blew the whistle wildly, and the helmsman on the wheel had not heard of it. The team could not stop it and had to fire a gun to warn them. Just when there was a commotion, the water police patrol team happened to be traveling from Huhu to Si on several towed boats of the Yutwu shallow water gunboat. Hearing the gunfire, the police suspected that it was bandits and fired at the shore, causing both sides to fire for half an hour. One policeman was accidentally killed. Later, the Home Guard knew that it was a misunderstanding and immediately signaled with a whistle. The water police also returned the signal and stopped fighting. The Home Guard team chief, Liu Jingsheng, boarded the ship and declared the misunderstanding to the water police. Unexpectedly, the water police did not understand and detained the team chief. At that time, villagers in various villages heard the alarm and gathered to help. The water police did not understand the truth and went ashore to arrest Zhou Songmin, the village chief of Yuantong Village, and villagers Qi Qisheng and Qi Afu, and took them to the Hongxingqiao team headquarters. It is reported that Zhou and others have been released on bail, but Liu Jingsheng is still in the team headquarters. The Yutwu ship has returned to Hu. The body of the dead policeman is parked in front of the ____ of the Xin Kaihe ____ Public Hall in this city and has not yet been coffined. After hearing the news, the Wu Xing County Government sent Secretary Tu to mediate. However, the navy has said that it will send Liu Jingsheng and team member Wang Achun to the province for interrogation.

The Provincial Minsheng Cotton Weaving Factory Closes: The Provincial Minsheng Cotton Weaving Factory, located in Qingyangdi, specializes in weaving various socks for export to foreign countries. The scale is very large, the number of people employed is quite high, and the expenses are very large. Manager Zhu Yushu resigned because the business was not prosperous and the capital was losing money. Before a year had passed, it was difficult to maintain. He had no choice but to submit a resignation to the province. The province ordered the county government to send someone to notify the closure and sent a commissioner to supervise the liquidation and hand over the factory by a deadline. It is reported that the factory only kept ten employees to handle the handover, and the remaining redundant personnel were dismissed. The factory's machinery and assets have been numbered and registered, and Shen Shichang, the chief of the Construction Section, has been inspected and is responsible for safekeeping.

County Police Force Implements Expansion: Due to rampant bandit-communists in Tongyi for years, the county police force's numbers were insufficient for allocation. The entire county's education conference has resolved to implement an expansion of two companies. This requires an additional 200 rifles, an initial operating fund of 40,000 yuan, and recurring annual expenses of 47,000 yuan.

Problem of Education Fees Collected with Salt Field Tax: Tongyi's salt fields total 12,225.11 mu. The education fee collected along with the land value tax is 6 fen per mu, but only 2 fen is actually collected. The county government has petitioned the province to increase it by 2 fen, which could yield an additional 24,450 yuan. This case requires verification and decision by the Transportation Bureau.

Rugao 87

Police and Militia Repel Haidao Pirates at Bencai: Pirate bandits from Bencai in Dongtai County are rampant. The county government ordered police officers from the Public Security Bureau and the First District Militia to suppress them. It is reported that the militia received a tip on the 1st at 10:00 AM that a large number of pirate ships were sighted at the 15th Zong, intending to land and plunder. Zhang, the Chief Inspector of the Public Security Bureau, and Geng, the instructor of the First District Militia, led a force of over a hundred men, along with Dongtai County police and the Bencai Militia, to encircle and suppress the pirates in two routes. They launched a fierce attack and engaged the pirates in a fierce battle for about three hours. Over twenty pirates were killed, and several pirates were captured. The pirates, unable to withstand the attack, collapsed and retreated in disorder. Three pirate ships and many items of clothing and ornaments were seized. One bugler sustained minor injuries. The local people are deeply concerned that the bandits will strike again and have specially requested that the police and militia remain to defend the area.

Gaoyou 88

Salt-Taizhou Steamer Encountered Danger: The Fuyong steamer of the Jiangtai Company, en route from Yancheng to Taizhou the other day, was suddenly surrounded by several pirate ships near Zhoujiazhuang in Taizhou territory, attempting to plunder it. Fortunately, there were over twenty members of the Provincial Water Police Team on board. Team leader Wang immediately led the team to engage the pirates in fierce battle, killing four pirates on the spot and capturing three alive. They were then escorted to the Taizhou garrison and handed over to the county government for legal proceedings.

Shangyu 89

Defeated Sheng Bandits Retreat to Their Old Nest: Bandits from Sheng County disturbed Tangtian, Hutang, Lizhou, and Beixi villages the previous month. According to reliable information, after the security teams from the four counties of Yu, Feng, Xin, and Sheng converged, they launched an attack at the end of the same month from Youzhuping, Jiangfan, Longxi, Pingkeng, Tangxi, and Lutian villages, guided by the militias. They advanced in the rain directly to Tangtian and engaged in a fierce battle. The bandits, unable to withstand the attack, retreated in disorder towards Chongren in western Sheng. Zheng, the company commander of the 11th Company of the 6th Security Regiment, believed that the villages had suffered greatly from the recent bandit disturbances. A prolonged presence of a large army would increase the burden on the people. Furthermore, the Sheng bandits had lost most of their strength and were unlikely to make a comeback. He entrusted the defense to the militias of the six villages, and the troops gradually withdrew to their original defenses. It is also reported that the villages adjacent to Tangtian, such as Dongjia'an, Yanxia, Chengda Keng, and Kaokeng, suffered the most intense bandit activity. People feared being burned and killed by the bandits, leading them to sleep in the open fields, and children dared not cry at night. It is still difficult to calculate the extent of the damage after being ravaged.

Kidnapping Case Occurs in Chelang Village: In Chelang Village, five li from Dongcheng, Che Kui, the nine-year-old only son of the late Che Peiling, was playing ball with his sister and aunt in the drying ground outside the gate after school at about 6:00 PM on the third. Unexpectedly, bandits suddenly arrived, kidnapped him, and fled. When the villagers heard the crying and rushed to the scene, the bandits fired a shot and fled through Lengshui Keng towards Baishi Ling. The city patrol team and the county defense team were notified and pursued, but there was no trace of them.

Important News

Zhongda Students Call on Education Minister 90

The Future University President Must Be an Ideal Figure

Nanjing, 6th - Student representatives from Zhongda (Central University) petitioned the National Government's Ministry of Education. The Ministry expressed sympathy for the students' opinions and swiftly dispatched President Jiang Menglin. The decision was to respect the students' opinions and ensure that the future university president would be an ideal figure.

The Zhongda Student Union will hold a by-election within two weeks of the start of the semester, as stipulated in its charter. It has been nine weeks since the semester began. On the 5th, a general student meeting of Zhongda resolved to suspend all activities of the current Student Union Executive Committee during the by-election period. On the 6th, the current Student Union issued a notice stating that when the fourth proposal was discussed at the general meeting, members gradually left the meeting, and the venue did not have a quorum. In accordance with Section 22 of the "Preliminary Steps in People's Rights," the fourth proposal was declared illegal. The Student Union will implement legal resolutions and deny illegal resolutions lacking a quorum. At the same time, it will submit a request to the National Government's Ministry of Education to accept the standards for the new president and swiftly appoint one. However, with the Zhongda students' general meeting denying the activities of the Student Union, a domestic dispute is imminent.

Detailed Record of Zhongda Student Congress 91

Yesterday's newspaper reported on the general outline of the student congress held on the afternoon of the 5th at Zhongda to discuss the president's issue. Here is a more detailed record of the meeting, divided into sections, to clarify the truth behind the student unrest.

Military and Police Authorities Closely Monitor 92

Since the Zhongda turmoil began, the Capital Garrison Headquarters has constantly dispatched detectives to monitor the situation at all times to prevent any reactionary elements. It was rumored that the authorities feared that some malicious elements might take the opportunity to disrupt order during the general student meeting held on the afternoon of the 5th. Therefore, on that day, fifty military and police personnel were dispatched to the venue to closely monitor and prevent accidents.

Discussion of Meeting Rules 93

Because there were so many people attending the general meeting, the Secretariat, which prepared for the general meeting, feared that the discussion of proposals would be chaotic and difficult to achieve results. Therefore, it posted slogans all around the venue, such as "Maintain Order in the Meeting," "Don't Give Outsiders a Pretext," "Discuss Personal Issues with Conscience," "Speak Calmly and Avoid Argumentation," etc. In addition, five special rules were discussed: (1) Each speaker may not speak more than three times on each proposal per month. (2) Each speech may not exceed five minutes, and the explanation of a proposal may not exceed ten minutes. (3) Amendments and temporary motions must be seconded by two or more people before they can be established. (4) Each proposal is passed if there is no objection after the chairman has seconded it twice. (5) No one may speak after the chairman announces the end of the discussion on each proposal.

Consolidation of Proposals 94

Several days before the meeting, the secretariat put up a notice to collect proposals from all students. The secretariat classified the proposals collected into eight cases as the basis for discussion at the meeting. Eight hundred and forty-four students attended the meeting. Before the meeting began, Chairman Tang Zuoquan took the stage and reported that there were 1,530 students in the school, and that the 844 students present constituted a quorum. He declared the meeting open. The chairman reported that the purpose of the meeting was threefold: (1) Since the launch of the school's reform movement, students have often made proposals for improving school affairs in the name of individuals or small groups, rather than the proposals of the entire student body. Improving school affairs is a matter of vital interest to the students. Today, we can take this opportunity to express everyone's opinions and consolidate them into the opinions of the entire Zhongda student body. (2) The community has paid close attention to the school's reform movement, and the news has been widely reported, but it is often inaccurate, leading to incorrect comments that are extremely detrimental to the school. Today, we must publish a declaration on the cases decided by the general meeting to correct the community's comments. (3) The successor to President Zhang has not yet been determined after his resignation. If the government does not resolve the president's issue quickly, it will affect the suspension and reorganization of the school. Therefore, this meeting is convened for detailed discussion.

Discussion Situation 95

During the discussion of the proposals, Liu Shichao chaired the first proposal: Should we express our attitude towards President Zhang's telegram to the faculty, staff, and students, expressing his firm resignation? The original proponent of the proposal, Jiang Xuegan, explained the reasons and content of the proposal, stating that he proposed that the school should use the name of the entire student body to send a telegram to retain President Zhang. If President Zhang does not come, we will discuss the successor candidate. After the explanation, most students opposed the proposal, saying that if we send a telegram to retain President Zhang, all past movements to improve school affairs would be meaningless. Furthermore, the facts prove that President Zhang has no possibility of returning to the school. "Resolution": No attitude will be expressed towards President Zhang's resignation. The second proposal resolves as follows: Given that President Zhang has expressed his intention to resign, the criteria for the successor should be determined as soon as possible to prevent ambitious people from coveting the position. Reason: The school resides in the capital and is the highest institution of learning in the country, bearing the responsibility of leading the national culture. The selection of the president should be particularly cautious. There are many people outside coveting the position. A single misstep would make future disputes even more unbearable. Survival and peril rest on this one move. The congress should determine the criteria for the successor candidate. Criteria: (1) One who enjoys high prestige for their scholarship and morality and has no bureaucratic habits. (2) One who can focus on their duties and has the determination and ability to develop Zhongda. (3) One who has achieved effective results in running higher education. (4) One who has a considerable history in the Party and the country. The third proposal was proposed by Zang Gonghui, Liu Maotang, and 54 others: The congress should propose a candidate for president based on the criteria for president and submit it to the government for selection and appointment. Candidates: (1) Yu Youren (2) Cai Yuanpei (3) Weng Wenhao (4) Hu Hanmin (5) Dai Jitao. After the proposal was made, most people believed that among the many talents in China, Zhongda's president could not be limited to the above five. Once proposed, it would be enough to cause misunderstandings and disputes in society and elsewhere. It is better not to propose. "Resolution": The entire proposal is rejected.

The fourth proposal was resolved and passed as follows: Please have the congress issue a declaration based on the following principles. Principles as follows: (1) The school is located in the capital and bears the mission of leading the national culture. The government should pay attention to the criteria for candidates as decided by the congress when selecting and appointing the successor president. (2) If the successor president does not meet the criteria decided by the congress, we vow to oppose them with all our might. (3) The students of the school will continue to attend classes with peace of mind and will not engage in any improper behavior. It is hoped that people in the community will not be misled by rumors deliberately spread by those with ulterior motives. (4) The school is responsible for the free and legitimate activities of external affairs groups. The congress generally denies anyone who pretends to be the official group or individual representing the entire school and any actions of the school's student union that violate the congress's resolutions. (5) The students of the school deeply believe that Party-based education will never violate Party doctrine.

Meeting Disruption 96

When the fourth [unclear character] was resolved, two students proposed a proposal: Students have been leaving the meeting one after another, and the meeting no longer has a quorum. According to the provisions of the "Preliminary Steps in People's Rights," the meeting should be adjourned immediately. Most students opposed this proposal, saying that those who attended the meeting and left voluntarily gave up their right to [unclear character]. The congress continued the discussion. Both sides argued fiercely. Some advocated changing to a talk show. Some asked the chairman to expel those few who were disrupting the order of the meeting. The atmosphere at the meeting was immediately tense. The Garrison Headquarters agents monitoring the scene immediately asked the chairman to stop the meeting to avoid disruption. Finally, those who questioned the number of people withdrew automatically, and the discussion of the fourth proposal continued.

The fifth, sixth, seventh, and eighth proposals argued that the matter was not an urgent matter and should be submitted to the next congress of representatives for discussion (the original proposals are attached). Now, a very important temporary motion is being discussed and resolved as follows: (1) The current Zhongda Student Union is not sufficient to represent the opinions of the entire student body. The school president's issue is of great importance. A special committee should be formed to represent the entire congress in handling all issues related to the new president, both internally and externally, until the new president arrives at the school. The special committee will then be disbanded. The special committee will consist of nine members elected by a vote of all students. Before the committee members are elected, the chairman of today's meeting, Tang Zuoquan, Liu Shichao, and Tu Juyao, will be responsible for all matters related to the drafting of declarations and elections. The direct meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

The four proposals left to be discussed at the next congress of representatives are as follows: (5) Reason: The school authorities are advised to establish a graduate school within the shortest possible time. Method: (1) Officially establish the graduate school this year and officially recruit graduate students in the summer vacation of next year. (2) Determine the funding for the graduate school: First, the additional funding of 120,000 yuan will be used as the graduate school's recurring expenses. Second, a portion of the funding for each school will be allocated to the graduate school. Third, submit a request to the government to specifically increase the recurring expenses of the graduate school. (3) Hire famous professors to guide research. (6) Reason: Request the school authorities to increase the number of free places and set aside a considerable amount of funding as a loan fund. (7)

) Reason: Request that the school authorities keep the library's McCoan Reading Room open all day during the winter vacation. (8) Reason: The congress should send someone to thoroughly investigate the various committees that used the school's name without anyone taking responsibility and issue a declaration to clarify the truth. Reason: The school has repeatedly discovered declarations and leaflets from the "Central University Nursing School Movement Committee" and the "Central University Anti-Traitor and School-Saving Committee" without anyone taking responsibility. To avoid misunderstandings from the outside world, we should thoroughly investigate and issue a declaration to clarify the truth.

Local News

Four District Party Headquarters 97

Declaration Against Encroachment on Educational Rights

The Public Concession's Municipal Council recently added an education department to investigate primary schools in the concession area and bring them under its jurisdiction, encroaching on China's educational rights. The Party Headquarters of the four districts of the city believes that this matter is of great importance to national rights and the future of education. It specially convened a meeting of all executive committee members yesterday to discuss the matter and resolved to notify all school principals in the district to hold an emergency meeting on a regular basis and issue a declaration to arouse the attention of all sectors of the city and the country and unanimously oppose it.

The declaration is recorded as follows:

Citizens of the whole city! Recently, the true face of imperialist cultural aggression has been glaringly exposed before our eyes. The concession authorities have established an education department and want to rule our national education within the concession. How ambitious is this ambition, and how seriously should we pay attention to it? We have three opinions to use as our cry in this declaration: First, we frankly and unceremoniously denounce the ambition of the concession authorities to establish an education department. Second, we want to promote the total awakening of schools in the concession to give the running dogs under the sphere of imperialist influence a stern warning. Third, we want to enable the citizens of the city to monitor the insane ambition of the concession authorities. Citizens of the whole city! This time, the concession authorities' measures have made us realize that imperialist arrogance is not retreating due to the rise of the world's small and weak nations, but is even advancing by retreating. It wants to use enlightened methods of plunder to divide the tide of national revolution. The concession authorities want to establish an education department to win over and numb the schools within the concession. This is indeed the best way to start. In fact, if we take a look at how many concessions there are in our country, once their ambitions are realized, we believe that bases for imperialist cultural aggression will spread throughout the country in a few years. Therefore, today, when national educational rights are unified, and when autonomy is complete, we do not need imperialism to divide our already unified educational rights. At the same time, under the complete autonomy of the nation, no ambition is absolutely allowed to devour any part of our autonomy. Citizens of the whole city, the fact is indeed the case. When imperialism wants to establish a concession education department to deceive us, we have indeed found that the past concession education was indeed extremely barren. This is the failure of those responsible for running education. Therefore, this has created such a situation. Imperialist aggression is "drilling where there is a hole" and "entering where there is no hole." The ambition to establish a concession education department originally saw that there was a hole to drill, so it became unstoppable. Therefore, the responsibility lies on the shoulders of the schools in the concession. They should recognize their own position and the nation's position to see through the intentions of the imperialists' measures and give the small running dogs of imperialism a serious warning on an orderly front. At the same time, for the sake of the non-unified educational rights of the nation, they should pay attention to everything in the future. Citizens of the whole city, since our territory has had a concession, it has been associated with so many sins, so much disturbance, and so much pain. The abyss of all evils is created intentionally by imperialism and its running dogs in the concession authorities. Recently, it has wanted to use the concession to encroach on our educational rights. It is a more enlightened but essentially more cruel hand. Citizens of the whole city, use our national wisdom to conquer the ambition of the concession authorities! Issued on November 6, year 19.

(3) The statement "Furthermore, the referee left the meeting without obtaining the opinion of our school, which is not the attitude that a referee should have" is even more incomprehensible. According to this article, the referee should have the right to stop the game without having to solicit the opinions of both parties. Special Note

Issues with the Education Department of the Concession (Zhou Shang) (Continued from Yesterday) 108

The Education Department has, in reality, been changed to the Education Office. However, the forms used for this survey of schools within the concession still boldly bear the title "Education Department." What is the reason for this? According to the Chinese Directors, the Concession Education Committee (details about this committee will follow) wishes to improve Chinese education and should first gather materials, follow scientific methods, proceed step by step, prescribe the right remedy, and then make improvements. Therefore, it was decided to survey schools within the concession, nominally under the "Shanghai Municipal Council Education Office." However, it was mistakenly written as "Education Department." Upon investigation, the mistake originated with the head of the Education Office, Healey, who approved the decision made by the committee. The Chinese members of the committee then questioned the authorities about this, nearly leading to a conflict. After a thorough investigation, it was discovered that the error lay with the secretary. Truly, a difference of a hair's breadth can lead to a loss of a thousand miles! A name represents an institution, and the matter is of great importance. If the Municipal Council mistakenly referred to itself as the National Government, how would the authorities rectify the situation? I secretly believe that the secretary should receive severe punishment, and the head of the Education Office should also offer a proper explanation.

Education Committee 109

The Chinese Directors of the Ratepayers' Association proposed reforms to Chinese education in the concessions. At the same time, they felt that the organizational structure of the Municipal Council's educational administration was flawed. Therefore, in March of this year, the "Education Committee" (Board of Education) was established, acting as an advisory body or a council. The resolutions of the committee are generally implemented by the Education Office. The committee members serve in honorary positions without stipends or remuneration. The aim is simply to reform education in the concession. Currently, there are seven members: three Chinese and four Westerners. Yuan Ludeng and Bell are ex officio members by virtue of being directors of the Ratepayers' Association. The remaining members are elected by the Chinese and Western directors of the Ratepayers' Association, respectively. Meetings are held every two weeks, with special meetings convened when necessary. In addition to the seven members, the Municipal Council's General Manager Edwards and the head of the Shanghai Municipal Council Education Office Healey attend the meetings. It is rumored that a Japanese person will soon join, but their name is not yet known.

Chinese readers are likely familiar with the qualifications of the Chinese members, so I will not elaborate. Regarding the backgrounds of the Western members, according to investigations, Shapard is affiliated with the church, Earl is a former professor at the University of Hong Kong, and Bell and Cela are both selected members. We should not ignore these facts. Furthermore, the proportion of Chinese members is only three out of eight, and no one is attending meetings. This seems unfair, and I sincerely hope that our Chinese Directors will strive to change this.

Since this committee is tasked with improving education in the concessions, what achievements has it made since its establishment? The establishment of elementary schools in the Western and Eastern districts, the purchase of school land worth over 400,000 yuan in Tilanqiao and near the North Station, the construction of housing for teachers and staff, and the planning of secondary schools are all among its accomplishments. However, many people are unaware of these things for reasons that are not yet fully clear.

Hopes for the Chinese Authorities 110

The failures of concession education are too numerous to list. The number of out-of-school children reaches over 150,000. Unscrupulous private schools inflict endless harm on young people. Pornographic and seditious publications, degrading plays and songs, gramophone records, opium dens, gambling establishments - all things that injure public morals and lead people into pitfalls - originate from the concessions. Before the right to education is recovered, we have the following hopes for the Ratepayers' Association and the Chinese members of the Education Committee:

(1) Urge the concession authorities to realize the situation and promptly return the right to education to us.

(2) Formally announce the abolition of the Education Department.

(3) The organizational structure of the Municipal Council's educational administration should be reported to the Chinese people immediately.

(4) If the Chinese members of the Education Committee face any difficulties, please explain them frankly.

(5) Demand that education funding account for 25% of the total revenue and guarantee its independence.

(6) If the objective cannot be achieved, the Chinese authorities may withdraw entirely to seek a solution. (The End)

Shen Bao National Industry and Commerce Conference Special Issue No. 7

Sixth Day of the Industry and Commerce Conference 111

Yesterday, the fifth general meeting discussed the review report of groups 1, 5, and 6. Important proposals such as promoting domestic goods, unemployment relief, and industrial and commercial relief were passed. The National Government was petitioned through the Ministry of Industry to vary the third phase of the commercial accounting period. It was resolved to approve the case that trade regulations must be uniformly followed by non-member firms in the same industry. The sixth and seventh general meetings will be held today, and the closing ceremony will be held tomorrow morning.

Yesterday's Fifth General Meeting

Reporting Circumstances 112

The National Industry and Commerce Conference continued its fifth general meeting at the Lishi Society yesterday afternoon from 1:00 to 5:00 PM. 133 members attended. The presidium included Hu Shuhua, Pan Gongzhan, Zhou Dian, etc. Professor Jian Xiangbiao from the Industrial College of the Central University also led 20 students from the mechanical and electrical engineering department to the meeting to observe. Chairman Kong Xiangxi announced the continuation of the fifth group review report. Shi Ying rose and said that before the report, regarding the review report of the fifth group, the reviewers had signed, but the original proposer was not listed. This was because one or two people were temporarily reviewing and signing to show responsibility, not that the entire review had been signed. Please do not misunderstand.

Discussion of the Fifth Report 113

Hu Shuhua reported the results of the fifth group's review of the third category, the promotion of domestic goods. There were a total of 19 proposals. Zhang Zilian said that it was difficult to collect goods for the domestic goods exhibition hall, and there were not many goods. The local government should buy the goods at half price, which would make collection easier.

Pan Xulun said that regarding the third point of the review report, regarding the user requesting the government to set an example for the people, the words "absolutely" not using foreign goods should be removed. The chairman said that he would pay attention to this point when organizing the entire case. Hu Shuhua said that this point was included in the detailed report. Huang Shoumin proposed that the entire review report on the promotion of domestic goods be passed. There was a seconded motion, and it was resolved that "the entire review report on the third case be passed."

The fourth category, industrial raw materials, was merged into the first category and reviewed and resolved to "pass."

The review report on the fifth category, industrial product standards, was completed. "The entire case passed." The review of the sixth category of other cases, except for cases 5 and 68, was resolved to pass.

Fifth Group Review Report

Discussions Yesterday 114

(Third Category) Promotion of Domestic Goods

Case 8: It is proposed to establish a state-run cigarette factory to recover rights. Case 38: It is proposed to establish a state-owned cement company to meet construction needs. The two cases were discussed together. "Resolved:" Please ask the government to first find ways to maintain private factories, so as to increase their development or encourage them to jointly operate to prevent infighting and strengthen their strength. As for the establishment by the state or joint government-business ventures, there are many obstacles, and it seems inconvenient to proceed at present.

Case 24: It is proposed that the Hubei Felt Factory, which promotes domestic goods, should be restored immediately to meet needs. Case 39: It is proposed to restore the Suqian Yaoxu Glass Factory to stop leakages. The above two cases were discussed together. "Resolved:" Please ask the government to consult with the provincial governments to invite merchants to contract for the operation, either by leasing or buying, with special concessions and proper protection and incentives, so as to quickly resume operations.

Case 43: It is proposed to establish a large-scale woolen weaving factory. Case 37: It is proposed to promote the national production of refined woolen clothing materials to recover rights. Case 60: Please set up a special woolen factory (additional proposal). Please build a large-scale woolen weaving factory along the Yellow River in the Northwest. The above four cases were discussed together. "Resolved:" (1) Location: choose one of the counties of Gaolan, Jingyuan, Zhongwei, Ningxia, and Pingluo in the Northwest to build the factory. In the Southeast, factories should be established in Guangzhou, Shanghai, Tianjin, and Fengtian. (2) Capital: Please encourage the people of the Southeast provinces to invest. The people of the Northwest have weak financial resources, so please ask the government to raise funds to establish the factory. (3) Raw materials: mainly local wool. (4) Products: first manufacture sturdy, timely, and applicable wool fabrics. (5) Sales: please order the military, police, students, and government employees to use domestic woolen cloth. (6) Improvement: Please have the Ministry of Agriculture and Commerce earnestly promote and incentivize the improvement of sheep breeds in the Northwest and Northeast. (7) Talent: Please have the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and the Ministry of Education consult and find ways to train more specialized wool manufacturing talent.

Case 6: Measures to promote domestic goods. Case 16: The Commodity Inspection Bureau should be affiliated with a commercial and industrial product exhibition hall. Case 23: It is proposed to rectify domestic goods to promote sales. Case 30: Establish a domestic goods market. Case 31: Procedures for promoting domestic goods nationwide. Case 41: Earnestly use domestic goods. Case 46: Committee for the promotion of domestic goods. Case 48: The "National Goods Trademark Compilation" should be widely reprinted and distributed by national commercial organizations to merchants to deeply educate the public and promote the sales of domestic goods. Case 55: It is proposed that the government find ways to promote domestic goods machinery and support the machinery industry. Case 61: It is proposed that the uniforms of the military, police, and various institutions and schools should use domestic goods, and all factories should be ordered to submit three fabric samples for selection. Case 66: Practical promotion of domestic goods to save the nation from crisis. The above eleven cases were discussed together. (1) Regarding taxes, please adopt a protective policy to exempt or reduce taxes on domestic goods, while increasing import taxes on foreign goods. (2) Regarding finance, please order domestic goods banks to lend money, limited to the domestic goods sector, and order all financial institutions nationwide to support domestic goods enterprises. (3) Regarding users, please have the government set an example for the people and absolutely not use foreign goods, and formulate regulations for the earnest use of domestic goods. (4) Regarding displays, please order the governments of all cities and counties to establish domestic goods exhibition halls. (5) Regarding awards, please have the government formulate award regulations to reward inventions of domestic goods and imitations of foreign goods. (6) Regarding marketplaces, please have the government order the governments of all provinces, cities, and counties to actively plan and establish domestic goods marketplaces and encourage them. (7) Regarding organizations, please have the government organize a committee to promote domestic goods and order the governments of all provinces, cities, and counties to jointly organize committees to promote domestic goods with local domestic goods manufacturers. (8) Regarding basic industries such as machinery manufacturing and livestock improvement, the people should strive to research and strive for progress, and the government should give special subsidies, awards, and guidance. (9) Regarding the cultivation of talent, please have the government encourage domestic goods factory owners to select personnel to study at home and abroad. (10) Regarding publicity, please have the government exempt taxes on domestic goods advertisements, and all domestic goods organizations and factories should pay attention to various publicity methods. (11) Regarding inspections, please order all bureaus not to be harsh, delay, or cause difficulties and extort.

Full Text of the Sixth Group Report 117

The conference submitted 25 proposals. Except for those that were transferred to other groups for discussion due to inconsistent nature, they are divided into two categories: (1) Unemployment relief (2) Industrial and commercial relief. For the convenience of the conference discussion, the already passed cases are summarized and reported as follows: Whether or not it is appropriate is still subject to public decision.

(1) Unemployment Relief Case 118

The unemployment situation in our country is becoming more and more serious. If no measures are taken to provide relief, it will become a source of social chaos. According to the cases, there are 21 methods: 1. Promoting domestic goods requires mandatory and permanent persuasion to enable the country to implement them effectively. 2. Laborers should not demand excessive wage increases, and capital should give bonuses as appropriate to realize labor-capital cooperation. 3. Clarify the boundaries between state-owned and private-owned to protect the position of investors. 4. All handicrafts are exempt from taxes to encourage them, and the National Goods Bank provides convenient methods for handicrafts (Note) "The above four articles are based on Article 2, Article 11, Article 15, and Article 28" 5. It is proposed that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce consider trying out the national introduction affairs bureau after the promulgation of the Vocational Introduction Law, but attention must be paid to talent training beforehand to avoid abuses (Note) "This article is based on Article 10 and Article 3 of Article 16" 6. It is proposed that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce consult with the Ministry of Internal Affairs, Agriculture and Industry to investigate the arable land in each province, declare them separately, and allow the people to migrate themselves (Note) "This case is based on Article 12 and Article 6 of Article 16" 7. Conduct unemployment registration and statistics on the overall unemployment situation. 8. Promote vocational education. 9. Develop industries. 10. Formulate unemployment insurance law (Note) "The above four articles are based on the resolution of Article 16" 11. Adopt a tariff protection policy. 12. Order existing factories not to experience work stoppages or strikes. 13. When factory goods are not selling well, the government will find ways to protect them. 14. Set up simple factories according to the market for goods (Note) "The above four articles are based on Article 18" 15. Revitalize water conservancy in the Northwest provinces (Note) "Based on Article 19" 16. Investigate the current state of occupations 17. Implement urban vocational guidance 18. Formulate laws and regulations for unemployment relief (Note "The above three articles are based on Article 20" 19. It is proposed that the government find ways to absorb overseas Chinese capital to develop industries 20. It is proposed that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce consult with the Ministry of Education to focus on industrial and commercial specialized subjects to increase skills (Note) "The above two articles are based on Article 24" 21. It is proposed that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce order all provinces to develop production and reorganize closed factories (Note) "This article is based on Article 25"

Appendix: Cases transferred to various groups Article 7 is transferred to the fifth group Article 8, items 1 and 2 are transferred to the fourth group Article 4 is transferred to the first group Article 9 is transferred to the fourth group Article 11, items 1 and 2 are transferred to the fourth group Article 4 is transferred to the third group Article 14 is transferred to the fourth group Article 20 is transferred to the fourth group Article 5 is sent to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for reference Article 26

(2) Industrial and Commercial Relief Cases 119

It is found that the precariousness of industry and commerce in our country urgently needs relief. The details have been described in detail in each case, and I will not repeat them. There are five areas and methods that should be rescued:

A. Relief methods for ordinary industry and commerce (1) The chambers of commerce in each place are responsible for informing each industry of their difficulties or successes and reporting them to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for separate awards and relief (Note) "This article is based on Article 1 and Article 4" (2) It is proposed that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce contact various industry groups in each province to elect representatives to organize a commercial maintenance committee, with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Finance, Transportation, Agriculture, Mining, Railways, and Railway as ex officio members to find ways to maintain (Note)

"This article is based on Article 6" (3) It is proposed that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce announce the boundaries of state-owned and private production to stimulate the people's interest in developing industries and to rescue the precarious industries (Note) "This article is based on Article 11" (4) All original factories in the country should be considered for exemption from commodity taxes to help them absorb raw materials so that their production increases and sales are smooth (5) The government should allocate capital to set up a model factory for various important industries to cooperate with merchants and people to advocate and know the joys and sorrows of industry and commerce and to absorb unemployed workers (6) The government should organize an industrial and commercial bank to allow the flow and relief of finances for industrial factories and reduce economic constraints (7) The government should follow Japan's example and hire experts to set up an industrial guidance agency to advise domestic entrepreneurs and make all facilities conform to scientific and economic principles (Note) "The above 14 articles are based on Article 22" (8) Follow the principle of the People's Livelihood to advocate and protect private enterprises to develop the national economy and save the crisis (9) Establish a state-run acid-alkali factory as soon as possible to promote the chemical manufacturing industry and return the industry (10 It is proposed)

Establish an international exchange mechanism as soon as possible to develop international trade and avoid being manipulated by foreign merchants in finance (Note) "The above three articles are based on Article 1, Article 2, and Article 3 of Article 25" (11) Focus on domestic and foreign surveys to promote the progress of national production (Note) "This article is based on Article 3 of Article 8" (12) Labor-capital disputes should be protected and mediated by the government (13) It is proposed that the central government order all provinces to cancel all harsh taxes and miscellaneous taxes (Note) "The above two articles are based on Article 17"

B. "Guangdong Silk Relief Methods" (1) It is proposed that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce suggest protective tariffs (2) It is proposed that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce allocate funds to relieve finances (3) It is proposed that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce coordinate foreign trade methods (Note) "These three articles are based on Article 3" C. "Methods to Relief the Rights of the Chinese Eastern Railway" (Note) "This article is based on Article 13" (1) It is proposed that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce consult with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Railways for handling

D. "Relief Methods for the Cigarette Industry" (1) Follow the example of the Zhang Yu Winery Company and allow Chinese cigarette factories to be exempt from taxes for ten years (2) If it is not possible to exempt all taxes, then 30% of the taxes payable by Chinese cigarette factories should be rewarded as in the past (Note) "This case is based on Article 23 and Article 30" E. "Relief Methods for the Tianjin Flour Industry" (1) Exempt domestic flour from special taxes and formulate foreign flour collection methods (2) If limited by the treaty, the same rate must be levied, and it is proposed to increase the import tax rate on foreign flour and reward domestic flour production as in the Shanghai example (Note) "This article is based on Article 31"

Pass the Sixth Group Report 120

After Pan Gongzhan finished reporting, the chairman asked to discuss the unemployment relief case first. Wang Xiaolai said that Article 12 of the review report ordered that existing factories should not experience work stoppages or strikes and should add malingering. Pan Xulun, Zhang Zilian, Shi Ying, and others advocated that there was no need for arbitration methods. Ding Jingchen said that this case was for unemployment relief and there were no regulations on work stoppages or malingering and advocated maintaining the original text. Pan Xulun said that this conference was not a way to raise funds and could not absolutely prohibit work stoppages, strikes, etc. and advocated that labor-capital arbitration should handle the matter. Wang Yunwu seconded Mr. Pan's proposal and added the words malingering to the original text.

Wang Jiean said that malingering is the cause of unemployment and the word malingering should be added. Mu Ouchu said that the original text added or malingering three words. Hu Shuhua advocated that Article 12 be cancelled and there should be no work stoppages, strikes, or malingering in the full text to avoid misunderstandings. Zheng Hongnian and others seconded the proposal and resolved that "Article 12 be revoked in full"

Pan Gongzhan continued to report the review results of the industrial and commercial relief case. Wang Ruoxi cancelled the full text of Article 12 on labor-capital disputes. Pan Xulun seconded the proposal and resolved that "passed" The chairman said that regarding the industrial and commercial relief case, if there were no differences other than Article 12, please raise your hands and resolve that "all passed"

If the national industry and commerce can unite and carry out the work, it may not be impossible in the future. It is proposed to send it to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for reference.

Article 40: Trade regulations that should be submitted to the competent official agency for approval should be uniformly observed by the same industry. Proposer: Shanghai Social Bureau Review results: Please forward it to the Judicial Yuan for interpretation by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce (all of the above passed)

Pass the case of approving trade regulations to be followed by the same industry

Pan Gongzhan, Wang Yansong, Wang Yunwu, and Wang Jiean vigorously advocated 122

Pass in principle and ask the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to adopt and implement

Next, the members discussed the trade association case, and the discussion situation was as follows:

The review results were reported by Wang Hantao. Wang Yansong believed that Article 40, proposed by the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau, stated that trade regulations of various industries that have been approved by the competent official agency should be uniformly observed by the same industry if they are not members of the association, was important and should ask the original proposer to explain the reasons.

Pan Gongzhan said that regardless of whether or not one joins a trade association, there should be no difference in trade regulations, otherwise those who join the association will uniformly abide by them, while those who do not join the association can change them at will. If the same industry is affected and the official agency's approval is ineffective, it will not be a blessing for industry and commerce. The trade regulations and industry regulations agreed upon by the same industry can supplement the shortcomings of the law and maintain the progress of commerce. For example, if the money industry association resolves on the daily foreign exchange rate, all industries in the city will uniformly abide by it, and there will be no monopolistic malpractices. If trade regulations cannot be consistent, the association will inevitably disintegrate. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce takes the trade associations of various industries as its basic associations. If it cannot maintain them, the General Chamber of Commerce will be difficult to isolate. The Social Bureau recognizes the importance of these trade regulations, so it proposed this case and asked everyone to discuss it.

Tian Jinbo said that the trade regulations vary from place to place. For example, trade associations in the interior often oppress small-scale operators. This case should be considered.

Wang Yansong said that the organization of the trade association and all the executive committees are composed of fair people elected by the same industry and there is no such thing as suppressing themselves, so there is no need to worry too much.

Mu Ouchu reported that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce had previously received the applications for record from hundreds of trade associations and the Social Bureau in Shanghai and had repeatedly discussed the matter with the competent department. It was felt that the trade regulations were indeed factual, but they conflicted with the law, so they were rejected.

Wang Yansong said that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce often handles commercial disputes based on the customary law of various industries. There have been no conflicts with the law in various processes. This time, the Shanghai Trade Regulations Maintenance Committee entrusted me as a representative, and my responsibility is great. Furthermore, the importance of party trade regulations has been explained by member Pan.

First Group, Second Review Report 123

Legislation to protect domestic nascent industries, limit speculation and price-fixing, and establish tariffs

Eliminate tax-free ports; ban the alteration of foreign products by changing packaging and trademarks to impersonate domestic products for mixed sale in the interior.

Change the third-period commercial accounting date; please request approval from the National Government

The received agenda is the third review report of the first group, covering twenty-six items from sixty-three to eighty-eight. The results of the review are as follows (numbering continues from the first time):

71. Proposal to protect the match industry by implementing a national match monopoly: passed.

72. Proposal to promote domestic goods with a systematic investigation: transferred to the fifth group for review.

73. Proposal to establish commercial arbitration offices: passed.

74. Proposal to revise exchange tax rates to use increased tax revenue to develop basic industries: transferred to the fourth group for review.

75. Proposal to restrict foreign merchants from establishing factories in China: to be handled together with Proposal No. 27.

76. Proposal to establish trademark registration sub-offices in various provinces and cities: to be sent to the Ministry for approval.

77. Proposal to eliminate tax-free ports and ban the alteration of foreign products by changing packaging and trademarks to impersonate domestic products for mixed sale in the interior: passed.

78. Proposal for state-owned property and state-run enterprises to be insured by Chinese insurance companies: to be sent to the Ministry for adoption.

79. Proposal to change the third-period commercial accounting date: upon investigation, the solar calendar accounting date was established by a clear order from the National Government; whether it can be changed should be submitted by the Ministry to the National Government for approval and implementation.

80. Proposal to negotiate and submit supplementary articles of the Chamber of Commerce Law to maintain the existing powers of local chambers of commerce: because the proposal involves amending the law, please have the General Assembly forward it to the Ministry for approval.

81. Regarding the difficulties arising from the joint and several liability for partnership businesses stipulated in the Civil Law, the speaker argued that after a vote in principle on this case, the legal aspects should be submitted by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to the Legislative Yuan to include this intention in the Trade Association Law.

Wang Xiaoxian stated that, according to Vice Minister Mu, the facts and the law often cannot be reconciled; he proposed that the Legislative Yuan should pay attention to the facts and include them in the regulations. Fang Jiaobo stated that the trade association's rules and the law do not conflict; the resolution of this case should be adopted and implemented by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and should not be included in the judicial scope.

Wang Jie'an stated that those who do not join the trade association may not comply with industry regulations, which is very harmful to the market; the Ministry of Industry and Commerce should be asked to adopt a resolution.

Hu Shuhua asked the chairman to stop the discussion and first vote on the principle of the case, and then ask the Judicial Yuan to interpret the legal aspects.

Fang Jiaobo stated that after the principle is passed, it should be handed over to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for handling, without the need for interpretation by the Judicial Yuan.

Wang Yansong seconded.

Wang Yunwu stated that trade association is necessary for the development of commerce. Those who have not yet joined the association should be persuaded to join. The resolution should only be handed over to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for handling, without the need for interpretation by the Legislative Yuan.

The chairman agreed with the trade association's rules, but the Legislative Yuan is in charge of the drafting of industrial and commercial laws and regulations, and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has no room for objection. The chairman proposed that the principle of this case be passed and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce be asked to adopt and implement it.

Pan Gongzhan stated that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce should be requested to approve the Legislative Yuan to change the law and include this article in the Trade Association Law.

Huang Shoumin advocated that the principle should be passed and the rest of the text should be discarded. Jiang Zudai seconded. Finally, the chairman passed the resolution to have the principle passed and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce adopt and implement it.

Please agree on supplementary articles to be forwarded to the Legislative Yuan for supplementary relief and sent to the Ministry to be forwarded to the Legislative Yuan for adoption.

Comfort Chairman Chiang and Comrades at the Front 127

Yesterday's temporary proposal

Yesterday, the General Assembly's temporary motion was to support the central government in suppressing the rebellion, consolidating peace and unity, protecting industry and commerce, and developing the economy. Please telegraph the whole country to clarify the righteousness of right and wrong, obedience and disobedience, and to comfort Chairman Chiang and the armed comrades at the front. The following measures were unanimously adopted: (1) The entire conference will telegraph Chairman Chiang and the armed comrades at the front to express their condolences, and telegraph the whole country to clarify right and wrong, obedience and disobedience, and to establish national policy. (2) The chairman of the conference will

lead everyone to stand in silence for three minutes to commemorate the wounded and dead soldiers at the front and express condolences.

Review by various groups yesterday 129

On the 6th, at 9:00 AM, the first, second, third, and fifth group review meetings were held at the Lizhi Society. The fourth group meeting was held at the Central Hotel, Room 318. The sixth group meeting was held at the Central Hotel, Room 268. Most of the proposals from various groups are expected to be reviewed by 12:00 PM. If there are any unfinished cases, they will be reviewed more intensively on the evening of the 6th to ensure that they are all completed and submitted to the General Assembly on the 7th for discussion and approval so that the meeting can be closed on schedule.

The proposal to establish an industrial and commercial bank was re-examined. Wang Yunwu talked about scientific management and the rationalization of national industries. He had previously been asked by the General Assembly to draft a complete proposal. He has now drafted a proposal for the Industrial Rationalization Research Committee, modeled after the German Industry Certification Design Committee. The drafting of this proposal has been completed and it can be reported at the General Assembly on the 6th. The method is to organize a national industrial rationalization research committee with the aim of planning a complete national economic research, organized by four types of groups and organizations: (1) central competent authorities and administrative agencies related to industry, such as the Construction Committee; (2) national academic groups, such as the Science Society, the Economics Society, the Industrial and Commercial Management Association, and the Engineering Association; (3) professional groups, such as the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce and the National Banking Association; (4) labor group representatives. Several experts will be hired by members to form a sub-committee to conduct detailed research on a certain issue. At the same time, because experts cannot be stationed at the association on a regular basis, a cadre department and a research department will be formed to handle all expenses. The central government is expected to allocate funds for this item.
