Zhang Linfei's Pigeon Dream 238

Encountered Adulterer Shan Xiaoxiong on the Road

Zhang Linfei, a lacquer worker from Pudong, is nearly thirty years old and still lives in poverty. Therefore, he searched everywhere for a good match as his wife. In September of this year, Mrs. Chen, who lives on Gonghe Xin Road, acted as a matchmaker, saying that her niece Chen Jindi, 22 years old, was a new widow who was seeking

Xiang Ru. The wealth and betrothal gifts were not a concern. At that time, both parties looked at each other and were both in their youth, so the matter was settled. The wealth and betrothal gifts only cost seventy-six yuan, and they immediately moved in together. On the third day of their wedding, a man suddenly came to visit, claiming to be Chen Xiaoxiong, Chen Jindi's brother. Zhang did not suspect him. Therefore, he came and went every day as if it were his own family. In fact, his real name was Shan Xiaoxiong, and he was Jindi's lover. He took this opportunity to continue their relationship. Zhang was still in the dark. However, the second landlord Jiang Hengdao was not deaf and had already learned the truth, but he did not interfere because it was none of his business. Unexpectedly, the day before yesterday, Jindi took seven pieces of clothing and twenty yuan in cash and ran away without a trace. Shan also disappeared. At the same time, Chen also moved away. Zhang lost both his wife and money, and the marriage, which lasted only two months, ended in a dream. He knew he had been deceived by a white pigeon. However, this white pigeon's design was to bring the adulterer into the home. He was deceiving people too much, so he searched everywhere. Yesterday, he encountered Shan Xiaoxiong on the road. The enemies met on a narrow road, and he brought him to the Second Section of the Fifth District and transferred him to the Local Court for questioning.

The Dispute over the Qiao Family Ancestral Temple

Qiao Yutang, a native of this county, currently residing at No. 67 Ju Men Road, Xieqiao, recently hired lawyer Jin Hongji to sue the woman Cao for illegally adopting a son-in-law to inherit the family lineage in the Local Court. He requested the court to investigate and make a fair judgment in accordance with the law to maintain the family lineage and avoid the chaos of a different surname inheriting the family line. He claimed that Qiao Yutang's ancestor, Duke Peilong, had two sons, the eldest being his late father, Guiqi, and the second being his late uncle, Guilin, dividing into two branches. Guiqi had two sons, the eldest being Atang and the second being the plaintiff Yutang. Atang also had two sons, the eldest being Rongsheng and the second being Linsheng (who had been adopted into the Zhang family). Yutang had two sons, Jingen and Wenbao. The second branch, Guilin, only had one son, Gengyu (Yutang's cousin). He lived with Cao (the defendant) as his wife for ten years and had no children. In the eighth year of the Republic of China, he adopted a daughter from the Zhu family in Lujiiawan, naming her Zhuying. Unfortunately, Gengyu died on July 21 of this year. The defendant unexpectedly recruited Gong Meisheng, Zhuying's fiancé, as an adopted son-in-law, naming him Jinde to inherit the Qiao family lineage. This time, after Gengyu's death, he used the name of the adopted son to issue a funeral announcement, excluding the uncles and nephews of the clan. He not only disregarded the ancestral temple but also violated the current laws. The most illegal thing was the pre-written will. On July 21 of this year, it was reported that lawyer Ye Fukang certified the will established by Qiao Gengyu and Qiao Cao, which was shocking. Gengyu died on July 21. It is questionable whether the will was established by Gengyu. Moreover, Qiao Gengyu had no children during his lifetime. According to current laws, those without sons are allowed to inherit from nephews of the same clan and generation. Therefore, Yutang's second son, Wenbao, should inherit the family lineage. Please make a fair judgment in accordance with the law, he said. The defendant Qiao Cao also filed a defense, saying that this will was certified by lawyer Ye and should be rejected the plaintiff's lawsuit, he said. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhao Zhenhai opened the court to conduct a collective hearing. The plaintiff Qiao Yutang, along with his sons Jingen and Wenbao, appeared in court. The defendant Qiao Cao also arrived as summoned. After the judge questioned both parties, he ordered both parties to go out and reconcile. If reconciliation fails, he will schedule another hearing to collect evidence.

Yang Family Property Dispute

Determining Identity and Attempting Reconciliation 239

In the case of Yang Rongfu from Chuansha suing the woman Gong Lu for occupying the inheritance of his adoptive father Yang Shiqiao in the Local Court and requesting a preliminary attachment, the court held a trial. The judge believed that the issue of inheritance could only be resolved after the identity was determined. Therefore, Yang withdrew the case and hired lawyer Liu Mingdu to file a succession lawsuit. The gist of the lawsuit is as follows: The plaintiff Yang Rongfu, 32 years old, from Chuansha, lives at No. 163 Dongjiadu, Yang Yichang Brown Mat Shop, and sues the defendant Gong Lu for occupying the inheritance of his adoptive father Yang Shiqiao (Yang Yichang Brown Mat Shop). He relied on inheritance to request confirmation of the inheritance in order to recover the inheritance. The plaintiff's father, Chun Qiao, and his brother, Shiqiao, had no sons. The plaintiff's father had two sons, the eldest being Ronghua and the second being the plaintiff Rongfu. From an early age, he went to his uncle's house. In the fourth year of the Republic of China, his aunt Zhou died, and the plaintiff wore mourning clothes in accordance with etiquette. All relatives and neighbors knew this. In December of the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, the plaintiff married and established a will as proof. Because his aunt died, his adoptive father lived with Gong Lu and repeatedly wanted to bring in Lu Taosen, the son of her previous husband, but was rejected by his adoptive father. On April 18 of this year, when his adoptive father died, the plaintiff was working in Hankou and rushed back to wear mourning clothes. There were no different opinions. Who knew that Lu was so eager to swallow the property that she secretly moved out the goods in Yang Yichang's shop? In desperation, he filed a lawsuit. The defendant Yang Lu (Gong Lu) also hired lawyer Tang Xingjian to file a defense, stating that in April of the fifth year of the Republic of China, she was married to Yang Shiqiao by matchmaker Gu of the Gu Shunxing Shop as his successor. The wedding was held in the Dongjiadu Catholic Church, and the priest witnessed the wedding. Since passing through the door, she had never seen the plaintiff. Her husband mentioned that he had a son named Asi who died of illness at the age of eight. There was also a nephew named Afu who did not work properly and idled around, so her husband did not allow Afu to enter the door. After her husband died, the plaintiff came to the store under the guise of care.

At first, he visited every day, then he brought his family to occupy the store. Finally, he took the store's business income at will and used it up, and slandered her with various foul words. The plaintiff's lawsuit should be rejected, she said. Yesterday morning, Judge Tong Shengli held a trial. Both parties, accompanied by their lawyers, appeared in court. The plaintiff Yang Rongfu stated the previous situation and said that all the documents had been submitted. The defendant claimed that she was Yang Lu, not Gong Lu. She was 54 years old, from Chongming. She was the successor of Yang Shiqiao. Lu Taosen was her adopted son and had no inheritance relationship with the plaintiff. According to witnesses Yang Ziqing, Hong Dalai, Yang Mao Da, and Huang Xishi, after testifying, the judge ordered the witnesses to mediate outside the court with a time limit of five days. If reconciliation failed, another hearing will be scheduled to collect evidence.

Zhang Huichong Debt Case Withdrawn 240

The case of film actor and underwater magic performer Zhang Huichong being sued by Zhong Caiji, Xie Qingzhang, and Jin Yu, the lawyer representing the Star Film Company, in the Shanghai Local Court to recover a debt of more than 3,800 yuan has been resolved peacefully with the mediation of friends such as Qiu Wanrong. Then he went to Xiamen to perform with more than 20 actresses such as Xu Su'e. However, the plaintiff also deposited 1,300 yuan in the court to provide security when requesting the attachment of the magic equipment. Now that the case has been resolved peacefully, yesterday the lawyers for both parties, Jin Yu and Shen Xingxia, jointly stamped and submitted a request to the court to withdraw the original case and requested that the silver and ocean dollars deposited by both parties be collected after settlement to complete the case.

Private Arms Trafficking Case Sentenced 241

Chen Qingyuan from Shantou, Lin Xinrui from Yong, Wang Yun and Wang A'er from Haizhou colluded to hide six box cannons, five pistols, and 475 bullets in the bottom of a net basket and in the compartment of an oil tank, and hired a car to send them to the Yuanyang Road Huishan Wharf on the morning of the 23rd of last month, intending to transport them to Shantou for profit. The case was discovered by Chinese and Western detectives from the Hongkou Patrol Division and the suspects, including Zhou Zicheng, an oil dealer, and Yu Shixian, a Qingkou resident, were arrested. The details of the case have been reported in this newspaper. Zhou Zicheng was found to be unrelated to the case and was released after the patrol division requested his release. The case has been concluded, and yesterday morning Judge Feng Shide declared the sentence in the Third Court: Chen Youyuan was sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment, Lin Xinrui was sentenced to four months of imprisonment, Wang Yun was sentenced to eight months of imprisonment, and Wang A'er was sentenced to four months of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the sentence was determined shall be offset by two days for each day of imprisonment. The five pistols, six box cannons, 475 bullets, one net basket, and two oil tanks were confiscated. Yu Shixian was found not guilty.

Correspondence 244

To the esteemed Editor:

With respect, I have recently read in the local news section of your esteemed newspaper an article about the lawsuit between Shen Xingtao and Han Qixiang over building a house being resolved out of court. This is not consistent with the facts. Upon investigation, the plaintiff originally filed the lawsuit first, and the defendant's address and the house being built are both located within the Public Concession. Therefore, it should be tried by the Special District Court, without the need for this lawyer to request a ruling. I immediately stated that the defendant's lawsuit in the French Municipal Council was filed later and could not proceed at the request of the defendant's lawyer in the French Municipal Council. If this case were to be tried in the French Municipal Council and a judgment were to be executed, the Special District Court would still need to provide assistance. However, according to Chinese national law, the Mixed Court is not recognized as a special court, and when Chinese executive authorities execute judgments of the Mixed Court, they cannot obtain the qualifications of Chinese executive authorities under national law, etc. Fearing that this would be misreported, I am sending this letter to request a correction. With best wishes for your well-being.

Yan Qing, Lawyer

November 6th

To the esteemed Editor:

With great respect, I have recently read in your November 6th newspaper that Li Yuankang, a shareholder of the Japanese Hongfu Company on Qipu Road, colluded with Bingyang, a fellow villager who had already been punished, on October 16th to sell counterfeit cigarettes, passing them off as Delong Company's Qimei cigarettes from North Henan Road. They were arrested by the French police and sent to the Special District Court for punishment, etc. Upon investigation, our company has no shareholder named Li Yuankang. Furthermore, this person had already published a statement on the 31st of last month declaring that Li Yuankang has no relationship with our company. Fearing that the outside world may not understand and that our company's business may be affected, I am sending this letter to you with the hope that you will allow us to make a correction. We would be extremely grateful. I respectfully submit this and wish you well.

Respectfully,

Lu Lianqing, Manager of Hongfu Company

Shanghai Market

Market News 245

Huanqiu Hat Factory at No. 516 Tiantong'an Gujiawan declares that their factory is a leader among Chinese-owned hat factories. They employ German technicians and purchase high-quality wool. From machine-made blanks to finished felt hats, everything is produced in-house, with no reliance on foreign sources. It is truly the most complete and flawless hat manufacturing operation in the country. Therefore, their products are excellent, and the prices are especially low. The distribution office is located at No. 66 Tianjin Road, and bulk buyers are rushing to purchase. In the midst of this movement to promote domestic goods, it is a particularly excellent phenomenon.

Since its establishment the year before last, the business of the Guohua Bank has developed at a rapid pace. Branch offices in various provinces have gradually expanded. In addition to the Hongkou and Xinzha branches in this city, a branch has also been established in the Nanshi area and opened yesterday. People from all walks of life came to congratulate, with a constant flow of vehicles and horses. It is reported that deposits of 60,000 to 70,000 yuan were received by the evening, which was quite a grand occasion for a time.

Theater News 246

The Zhabei Gengxin Stage declares that it has been performing "Journey to the West, Part Two" for over two months. Because the play has many scenes with bizarre, novel, and unique mechanical sets, and the scene of the哮天犬 (Xiàotiānquǎn, Howling Celestial Dog) chasing and biting Sun Wukong, the dog is no less impressive than the foreign Ling Ding Ding, it is extremely popular among audiences and is almost always sold out every night. Recently, the owner, Mr. Zhou Xiaoqing, in order to refresh the audience's senses, has specially added exciting elements to scenes such as dancing in Part Two, further increasing the audience.

The Wuchang Grand Theater declares that it will begin showing the famous aviation revenge film "Airplane War" and the film "Bastard Prince" starring Locke, starting today. One is passionate and stirring, and the other is humorous and absurd.

The Xinghua Music and Dance Society declares that the society was founded by playwrights Fu Jinming and Shen Guangle and has been in preparation for more than two months. Yesterday, the society held its inaugural meeting in the auditorium of the 14th branch of the Xiaonanmen district. A total of more than 40 guests and members attended. After the ceremony, in addition to electing the various officers, it was also decided to recruit members. Those from all walks of life who are interested in joining (can directly contact the society at No. 6, Lane 207, Yanhai Road in the city). Brochures are available upon request.

Ruilong Company declares that the company's recently produced martial arts adventure comedy giant film "The Four Heroes of the East" has a bizarre and convoluted plot, with extraordinary adventures, and is interspersed with humorous actions that can make people laugh through tears, which is a creation in domestic films. The structure is excellent and unexpected. The film is directed by Mr. Ren Pengnian and stars Cha Ruilong, Wu Lizhu, Wang Dongxia, etc. The photography is handled by the experienced Ren Pengshou, so the lighting is very accurate, and the shooting method is also very novel. Interior scenes were being filmed yesterday and should be completed soon.

Lonely Star Film Company declares that the company's recently filmed drama "Yangtze River" is a great social, emotional, and revolutionary film that has now been fully completed. The plot is very convoluted, and the actors are all selected from the company's best, such as Qian Siying, Lu Fuyao, and Bao Gusong, who all play important roles in the film. It will premiere at the Central Grand Theater in this city soon. The company has been working day and night to produce films. The play "Jin Tai Zhuan," directed by Lu Yeyuan, has been fully prepared. Next week, Director Lu will lead the full cast and crew to shoot exterior scenes.

Star Film Company declares that the company and the Public Voice Film Company are producing two major domestic sound films. One is the opera film "Singing Girl Red Peony," starring Hu Die, which has been in production for more than four months and is two-thirds completed. The other is the martial arts film "Robber Son," starring Wang Yuanlong, which has been in production for one-third. Both films are directed by Zhang Shichuan, who is working day and night, sparing no effort, hoping to complete them as soon as possible to meet the expectations of society.

Medical News 247

The Shanghai YMCA declares that its First Aid Trauma Class is held to prevent unforeseen dangers. It is taught by surgeon Pan Fuyin, the current director of the Chinese Leprosy Hospital. Classes are held for two hours each week and completed in ten weeks. A certificate will be issued upon graduation. The quota is 30 students, but there are already more than 40 applicants. In order to satisfy the eagerness of those seeking knowledge, the limit has been broken, and it is planned to open another class for those who continue to apply in the future.

The Yuqingfang Youth Traditional Chinese Medicine Society on North Sichuan Road declares that the number of subscribers to the "Modern Famous Doctors' Veritable Case Studies" published by the society is increasing daily, because the content is becoming more and more refined and the notes are recorded truthfully, which can be used for both novel reading and medical book reading. The most recent fourth issue contains many cases of venereal diseases, from onset to cure, strange and unusual, treated and cured by a certain doctor with a name and address, which is not comparable to fabricated stories. Currently, for popularization purposes, all four volumes are sold for 20 cents, and the full year is one yuan.
